def test_hdp_ecomm_h_edit_cancel(self, merchant_login, cs_login, sh_login):
"""
即收即送到家单-截单前修改订单寄件/派件时间、寄件/收件人、电话，派件地址、货物重量、箱大小、箱数，排线成功后取消订单
:return:
"""
merchant = merchant_login # 初始化商家并登陆
cs = cs_login
sh = sh_login

# 商家下单，返回订单号，包收地址时间段，包派地址时间段

# 获取营运点

sh.sh_delivery_search_result(to_sh_id, order_sn, delivery="1") # 检查待派件表

# 设置修改订单资料

total_weight = _weigth

sender_phone = "98912345"
recipient_name = "recipient_test"
recipient_phone = "98212345"
cs.CsHomeExpress_edit_order(order_sn, total_weight=total_weight, box_size_code=box_size_code,
box_quantity=box_quantity, recipient_address=recipient_address,
sender_name=sender_name, sender_phone=sender_phone, pickup_time="edit",
recipient_name=recipient_name, recipient_phone=recipient_phone) # 修改订单派件地址

assert od_if["box_qty"] == box_quantity

@allure.feature('homeexpress_sh_sp_operator')
@allure.severity('normal')
@allure.story('test_hdp_sfwh_h_order_freeze_unfreeze')
def test_hdp_sfwh_h_order_freeze_unfreeze(self, merchant_login, cs_login, sh_login, home_tasker_login):
"""
仓库即送到家单，冻结-解冻流程
:return:
"""
merchant = merchant_login # 初始化商家并登陆
cs = cs_login
sh = sh_login
tasker = home_tasker_login

# 商家下单，返回订单号，包收地址时间段，包派地址时间段
product_code = "HDP-SFWH-H" # 仓库即送到家
cs.change_product_home(product_code, merchant.merchant_id)
order_id_list, address, datetime = merchant.merchant_warehouse_add_order(product_code=product_code, cs=cs)
order_sn = order_id_list[0]

# 获取营运点
from_sh_id, to_sh_id = sh.get_order_sh_id(address, datetime, product_code)

sleep(2)
sh.sh_pickup_search_result(from_sh_id, order_sn, pickup="2") # 检查待收件表
sh.sh_delivery_search_result(to_sh_id, order_sn, delivery="1") # 检查待派件表

# 冻结订单
merchant.SFCommon_mock_test(order_sn) # 底层API触发冻结请求
sh.businessorder_in_storage(order_sn, from_sh_id) # 货件入仓
# datetime = merchant.get_order_time(order_id_list, datetime) # 更新订单时间
sh.sh_item_search_result(from_sh_id, order_sn) # 检查起点营运点仓存表
sh.businessorder_freeze(waybill_no=order_sn, hub_id=from_sh_id) # 冻结扫码
sleep(5)
cs.cshomeexpress_get_order_info(order_sn, state_code="9042") # 检查订单状态，9042已冻结
sh.sh_item_search_result(from_sh_id, order_sn, item_status="10", route_status="2") # 冻结状态，已取消
sh.sh_pickup_search_result(from_sh_id, order_sn, route_status="2") # 已取消
sh.sh_delivery_search_result(to_sh_id, order_sn, route_status="2") # 已取消

# 解冻订单，生成新单
new_order_sn, new_order_datetime = cs.Cs_HomeExpress_create_order(order_sn=order_sn, product_code=product_code,
remark="测试-解冻订单",
csremark="测试-客服CS解冻订单") # CS后台操作解冻触发解冻特殊操作请求
sleep(3)
sh.BusinessOrder_unfreeze(waybill_no=order_sn, hub_id=from_sh_id) # 解冻扫码
sleep(5)
cs.cshomeexpress_get_order_info(new_order_sn, state_code="9015") # 检查新单状态，9015运送中
res_item = sh.sh_item_search_result(from_sh_id, new_order_sn, item_status="1", route_status="0")
assert res_item[0]["waybill_no"] == order_sn
res_pickup = sh.sh_pickup_search_result(from_sh_id, new_order_sn, route_status="2")
assert res_pickup[0]["waybill_no"] == order_sn
resp_delivery = sh.sh_delivery_search_result(to_sh_id, new_order_sn, route_status="0")
assert resp_delivery[0]["delivery"] == "1"

# 完成派程
sh.sh_confirm_route_plans(order_id_list, from_sh_id, to_sh_id, "2", new_order_datetime,
partner_id=tasker.tasker_id)
tasker.tasker_force_set_work_position_online(van_position, cs) # 配送员上线
sh.businessorder_out_result(order_sn, to_sh_id) # 出仓扫码
group_id, order_id, pickup_code = cs.get_order_info("delivery", order_sn=new_order_sn)
assert cs.get_wait_task_state(order_id, "413")
home.home_delivery_overflow(order_id, "911", merchant, tasker, cs, normal_appeal=True,
location_appeal=True) # 完成包派单
